    'Anja Mller-Schache (born 29 March 1977) is a German foil fencer\n' +
    '[/wiki/Foil_fencer].[2] She won a bronze medal, as a member of the German\n' +
    'fencing team, at the 2009 World Fencing Championships\n' +
    '[/wiki/2009_World_Fencing_Championships] in Antalya, Turkey\n' +
    '[/wiki/Antalya,_Turkey].[3]\n' +
    '\n' +
    'Schache represented Germany [/wiki/Germany] at the 2008 Summer Olympics\n' +
    '[/wiki/2008_Summer_Olympics] in Beijing [/wiki/Beijing], where she competed in\n' +
    "two foil events. For her first event, the women's individual foil\n" +
    '[/wiki/Fencing_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_foil], Schache\n' +
    'received a bye for the second preliminary round match, before losing out to\n' +
    "Russia's Evgenia Lamonova [/wiki/Evgenia_Lamonova], with a score of 215.[4] Few\n" +
    'days later, she joined with her fellow fencers and teammates Melanie Wolgast,\n' +
    'Katja Wchter [/wiki/Katja_W%C3%A4chter], and Carolin Golubytskyi\n' +
    "[/wiki/Carolin_Golubytskyi] for the women's team foil\n" +
    '[/wiki/Fencing_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_team_foil].\n' +
    'Schache and her team, however, lost the fifth place match to the Chinese team\n' +
    '(led by Zhang Lei [/wiki/Zhang_Lei_(fencing)]), with a total score of 28\n' +
    'touches.[5]\n' +
    '\n' +
    '\n' +
